Input Artifacts:
  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.   - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.   - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.   - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.   - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.   - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.   - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.  ### 2. Device List Page - **Page Title**: My Devices - **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls. - **Elements**:   - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.   - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.   - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Add Device Page - **Page Title**: Add New Device - **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device. - **Elements**:   - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.   - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.   - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).   - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).   - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 4. Device Control Page - **Page Title**: Device Control - **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings. - **Elements**:   - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.   - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.   - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).   - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.   - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.   - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.  ### 5. Automation Rules Page - **Page Title**: Automation Rules - **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.   - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.   - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.   - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).   - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).   - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.   - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).   - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. Energy Report Page - **Page Title**: Energy Report - **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.   - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.   - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.   - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.   - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Activity Logs Page - **Page Title**: Activity Logs - **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events. - **Elements**:   - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.   - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.   - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.   - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com   jane_smith|jane@example.com   ```  ### 2. Device Data - **File Name**: `devices.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|   john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00   jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|   ```  ### 3. Room Data - **File Name**: `rooms.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|room_id|room_name   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room   john_doe|2|Bedroom   john_doe|3|Kitchen   jane_smith|1|Living Room   ```  ### 4. Automation Rules Data - **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true   john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true   jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true   ```  ### 5. Energy Consumption Logs - **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5   john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3   john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6   jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2   ```  ### 6. Activity Logs - **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|timestamp|device_id|action|details   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights   john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72   jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

Data Schemas\n\n### users.txt\nFormat:\n```\nusername|email\n```\nExample:\n```\njane_smith|jane@example.com\n```\n\n### devices.txt\nFormat:\n```\nusername|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time\n```\nExample:\n```\njohn_doe|1|Living Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|\n```\n\nNotes:\n- status: Online/Offline\n- power: on/off\n- brightness, temperature are integers or empty\n- mode: string\n- schedule_time: string or empty\n\n### rooms.txt\nFormat:\n```\nusername|room_id|room_name\n```\nExample:\n```\njohn_doe|1|Living Room\njohn_doe|2|Bedroom\n```\n\n### automation_rules.txt\nFormat:\n```\nusername|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled\n```\nExample:\n```\njohn_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true\njane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true\n```\nNotes:\n- enabled is boolean string 'true' or 'false'\n\n### energy_logs.txt\nFormat:\n```\nusername|device_id|date|energy_consumed\n```\nExample:\n```\njohn_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5\njohn_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3\n```\n\n### activity_logs.txt\nFormat:\n```\nusername|timestamp|device_id|action|details\n```\nExample:\n```\njohn_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power Changed|Morning Lights\njohn_doe|2024-11-01 07:10:00|1|Temperature Changed|to 22C\n```\n\n## 5. Naming Conventions\n\n- Element IDs use lowercase with hyphens\n- Dynamic IDs include entity and id, e.g., control-device-button-{device_id}\n- Flask function names use snake_case descriptive form\n\n## Summary\nThis design specification covers the web routes, templates including page titles and element IDs, navigation mapping, and the data schemas for local storage files under `data/` directory. It ensures consistent and precise design for frontend development working independently as the single source of truth."})

Routing and Endpoints  ### Base URL Redirect - `/` redirects to `/dashboard`  ### Device Endpoints - `/devices` - List all devices - `/devices/add` - Add new device - `/devices/<int:device_id>` - Control individual device  ### Automation Endpoints - `/automation` - List and manage automation rules  ### Reports and Activity Logs - `/reports` - View energy consumption reports - `/activity` - View device activity logs  ## 2. Flask Function and Route Naming  | Function Name        | Route                  | Description                           | |----------------------|------------------------|-----------------------------------| | `redirect_to_dashboard` | `/`                    | Redirects to Dashboard             | | `dashboard_page`     | `/dashboard`           | Shows dashboard overview           | | `list_devices`       | `/devices`             | Lists devices                      | | `add_device`         | `/devices/add`         | Adds new device                    | | `control_device`     | `/devices/<int:device_id>` | Device control page                | | `automation_page`    | `/automation`          | Shows automation rules             | | `reports_page`       | `/reports`             | Energy consumption reports         | | `activity_page`      | `/activity`            | Device activity logs               |  ## 3. control-device-button-{device_id} (dynamic) -> route `control_device` with device_id  ### Add Device Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/add.html - **Page Title (h1)**: New Device - **Container ID**: add-device-page - cancel-button -> route `list_devices`  ### Device Control Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/control.html - **Page Title (h1)**: Device Control - **Container ID**: control-device-page - **Elements:**   - Button: toggle-power-button-{device_id}   - Button: save-settings-button   - Button: back-to-devices-button -> route `list_devices`  ### Automation Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/automation.html - action-type-select   - Button: add-rule-button   - Button: save-rules-button  ### Reports Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/reports.html - **Page Title (h1)**: Energy Consumption Report - **Container ID**: energy-page - **Elements:**   - Summary: energy-summary   - Date input: filter-date-input   - Button: apply-filter-button   - Button: dashboard-button -> `dashboard_page`  ### Activity Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/activity.html - **Page Title (h1)**: Activity Logs - **Container ID**: activity-page - **Elements:**   - Table: activity-logs-table   - Input: search-input   - Button: search-button   - Button: clear-button  ## 4. Data Schemas  ### users.txt Format: ``` username|email ``` Example: ``` jane_smith|jane@example.com ```  ### devices.txt Format: ``` username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time ``` Example: ``` john_doe|1|Living Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto| ```  Notes: - status: Online/Offline - power: on/off - brightness, temperature are integers or empty - mode: string - schedule_time: string or empty  ### rooms.txt Format: ``` username|room_id|room_name ``` Example: ``` john_doe|1|Living Room john_doe|2|Bedroom ```  ### automation_rules.txt Format: ``` username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled ``` Example: ``` john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true ``` Notes: - enabled is boolean string 'true' or 'false'  ### energy_logs.txt Format: ``` username|device_id|date|energy_consumed ``` Example: ``` john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5 john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3 ```  ### activity_logs.txt Format: ``` username|timestamp|device_id|action|details ``` Example: ``` john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power Changed|Morning Lights john_doe|2024-11-01 07:10:00|1|Temperature Changed|to 22C ```  ## 5. Naming Conventions  - Element IDs use lowercase with hyphens - Dynamic IDs include entity and id, e.g., control-device-button-{device_id} - Flask function names use snake_case descriptive form  ## Summary This design specification covers the web routes, templates including page titles and element IDs, navigation mapping, and the data schemas for local storage files under `data/` directory. It ensures consistent and precise design for frontend development working independently as the single source of truth.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.


=== design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

## 1. Routing and Endpoints

### Base URL Redirect
- `/` redirects to `/dashboard`

### Device Endpoints
- `/devices` - List all devices
- `/devices/add` - Add new device
- `/devices/<int:device_id>` - Control individual device

### Automation Endpoints
- `/automation` - List and manage automation rules

### Reports and Activity Logs
- `/reports` - View energy consumption reports
- `/activity` - View device activity logs

## 2. Flask Function and Route Naming

| Function Name        | Route                  | Description                           |
|----------------------|------------------------|-----------------------------------|
| `redirect_to_dashboard` | `/`                    | Redirects to Dashboard             |
| `dashboard_page`     | `/dashboard`           | Shows dashboard overview           |
| `list_devices`       | `/devices`             | Lists devices                      |
| `add_device`         | `/devices/add`         | Adds new device                    |
| `control_device`     | `/devices/<int:device_id>` | Device control page                |
| `automation_page`    | `/automation`          | Shows automation rules             |
| `reports_page`       | `/reports`             | Energy consumption reports         |
| `activity_page`      | `/activity`            | Device activity logs               |

## 3. Page Templates Details

### Dashboard Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/dashboard.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Overview
- **Container ID**: dashboard-page
- **Elements:**
  - Summary Divs:
    - device-summary (shows total devices, online, offline counts)
  - Buttons:
    - automation-button -> route `automation_page`
    - energy-button -> route `reports_page`
    - devices-button -> route `list_devices`

### My Devices Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/list.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: My Devices
- **Container ID**: devices-list-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table with ID: device-table
  - Buttons:
    - add-device-button -> route `add_device`
    - control-device-button-{device_id} (dynamic) -> route `control_device` with device_id

### Add Device Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/add.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: New Device
- **Container ID**: add-device-page
- **Elements:**
  - Dropdown select: device-type-select (options: Camera, Sensor, Light, Thermostat)
  - Dropdown select: room-select
  - Input: device-name-input
  - Buttons:
    - save-device-button
    - cancel-button -> route `list_devices`

### Device Control Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/control.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Device Control
- **Container ID**: control-device-page
- **Elements:**
  - Button: toggle-power-button-{device_id}
  - Button: save-settings-button
  - Button: back-to-devices-button -> route `list_devices`

### Automation Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/automation.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Automation
- **Container ID**: automation-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table: rules-table
  - Inputs:
    - rule-name-input
    - trigger-type-select
    - trigger-value-input
    - target-device-select
    - action-type-select
  - Button: add-rule-button
  - Button: save-rules-button

### Reports Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/reports.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Energy Consumption Report
- **Container ID**: energy-page
- **Elements:**
  - Summary: energy-summary
  - Date input: filter-date-input
  - Button: apply-filter-button
  - Button: dashboard-button -> `dashboard_page`

### Activity Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/activity.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Activity Logs
- **Container ID**: activity-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table: activity-logs-table
  - Input: search-input
  - Button: search-button
  - Button: clear-button

## 4. Data Schemas

### users.txt
Format:
```
username|email
```
Example:
```
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### devices.txt
Format:
```
username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|Living Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
```

Notes:
- status: Online/Offline
- power: on/off
- brightness, temperature are integers or empty
- mode: string
- schedule_time: string or empty

### rooms.txt
Format:
```
username|room_id|room_name
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
```

### automation_rules.txt
Format:
```
username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```
Notes:
- enabled is boolean string 'true' or 'false'

### energy_logs.txt
Format:
```
username|device_id|date|energy_consumed
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
```

### activity_logs.txt
Format:
```
username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
```
Example:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power Changed|Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:10:00|1|Temperature Changed|to 22C
```

## 5. Naming Conventions

- Element IDs use lowercase with hyphens
- Dynamic IDs include entity and id, e.g., control-device-button-{device_id}
- Flask function names use snake_case descriptive form

## Summary
This design specification covers the web routes, templates including page titles and element IDs, navigation mapping, and the data schemas for local storage files under `data/` directory. It ensures consistent and precise design for frontend development working independently as the single source of truth.

**Elements:**   - Dropdown select: device-type-select (options: Camera, Sensor, Light, Thermostat)   - Dropdown select: room-select   - Input: device-name-input   - Buttons:     - save-device-button     - cancel-button -> route `list_devices`  ### Device Control Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/control.html - **Page Title (h1)**: Device Control - **Container ID**: control-device-page - **Elements:**   - Button: toggle-power-button-{device_id}   - Button: save-settings-button   - Button: back-to-devices-button -> route `list_devices`  ### Automation Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/automation.html - action-type-select   - Button: add-rule-button   - Button: save-rules-button  ### Reports Page - **Template Filepath**: templates/reports.html - **Page Title (h1)**: Energy Consumption Report - **Container ID**: energy-page - Naming Conventions  - Element IDs use lowercase with hyphens - Dynamic IDs include entity and id, e.g., control-device-button-{device_id} - Flask function names use snake_case descriptive form  ## Summary This design specification covers the web routes, templates including page titles and element IDs, navigation mapping, and the data schemas for local storage files under `data/` directory. It ensures consistent and precise design for frontend development working independently as the single source of truth.

INPUT: === user_task_description ===

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.


=== design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

## 1. Routing and Endpoints

### Base URL Redirect
- `/` redirects to `/dashboard`

### Device Endpoints
- `/devices` - List all devices
- `/devices/add` - Add new device
- `/devices/<int:device_id>` - Control individual device

### Automation Endpoints
- `/automation` - List and manage automation rules

### Reports and Activity Logs
- `/reports` - View energy consumption reports
- `/activity` - View device activity logs

## 2. Flask Function and Route Naming

| Function Name        | Route                  | Description                           |
|----------------------|------------------------|-----------------------------------|
| `redirect_to_dashboard` | `/`                    | Redirects to Dashboard             |
| `dashboard_page`     | `/dashboard`           | Shows dashboard overview           |
| `list_devices`       | `/devices`             | Lists devices                      |
| `add_device`         | `/devices/add`         | Adds new device                    |
| `control_device`     | `/devices/<int:device_id>` | Device control page                |
| `automation_page`    | `/automation`          | Shows automation rules             |
| `reports_page`       | `/reports`             | Energy consumption reports         |
| `activity_page`      | `/activity`            | Device activity logs               |

## 3. Page Templates Details

### Dashboard Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/dashboard.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Overview
- **Container ID**: dashboard-page
- **Elements:**
  - Summary Divs:
    - device-summary (shows total devices, online, offline counts)
  - Buttons:
    - automation-button -> route `automation_page`
    - energy-button -> route `reports_page`
    - devices-button -> route `list_devices`

### My Devices Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/list.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: My Devices
- **Container ID**: devices-list-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table with ID: device-table
  - Buttons:
    - add-device-button -> route `add_device`
    - control-device-button-{device_id} (dynamic) -> route `control_device` with device_id

### Add Device Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/add.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: New Device
- **Container ID**: add-device-page
- **Elements:**
  - Dropdown select: device-type-select (options: Camera, Sensor, Light, Thermostat)
  - Dropdown select: room-select
  - Input: device-name-input
  - Buttons:
    - save-device-button
    - cancel-button -> route `list_devices`

### Device Control Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/devices/control.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Device Control
- **Container ID**: control-device-page
- **Elements:**
  - Button: toggle-power-button-{device_id}
  - Button: save-settings-button
  - Button: back-to-devices-button -> route `list_devices`

### Automation Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/automation.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Automation
- **Container ID**: automation-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table: rules-table
  - Inputs:
    - rule-name-input
    - trigger-type-select
    - trigger-value-input
    - target-device-select
    - action-type-select
  - Button: add-rule-button
  - Button: save-rules-button

### Reports Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/reports.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Energy Consumption Report
- **Container ID**: energy-page
- **Elements:**
  - Summary: energy-summary
  - Date input: filter-date-input
  - Button: apply-filter-button
  - Button: dashboard-button -> `dashboard_page`

### Activity Page
- **Template Filepath**: templates/activity.html
- **Page Title (h1)**: Activity Logs
- **Container ID**: activity-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table: activity-logs-table
  - Input: search-input
  - Button: search-button
  - Button: clear-button

## 4. Data Schemas

### users.txt
Format:
```
username|email
```
Example:
```
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### devices.txt
Format:
```
username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|Living Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
```

Notes:
- status: Online/Offline
- power: on/off
- brightness, temperature are integers or empty
- mode: string
- schedule_time: string or empty

### rooms.txt
Format:
```
username|room_id|room_name
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
```

### automation_rules.txt
Format:
```
username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```
Notes:
- enabled is boolean string 'true' or 'false'

### energy_logs.txt
Format:
```
username|device_id|date|energy_consumed
```
Example:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
```

### activity_logs.txt
Format:
```
username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
```
Example:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power Changed|Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:10:00|1|Temperature Changed|to 22C
```

## 5. Naming Conventions

- Element IDs use lowercase with hyphens
- Dynamic IDs include entity and id, e.g., control-device-button-{device_id}
- Flask function names use snake_case descriptive form

## Summary
This design specification covers the web routes, templates including page titles and element IDs, navigation mapping, and the data schemas for local storage files under `data/` directory. It ensures consistent and precise design for frontend development working independently as the single source of truth.

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.   - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.   - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.   - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.   - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.   - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.   - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.  ### 2. Device List Page - **Page Title**: My Devices - **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls. - **Elements**:   - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.   - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.   - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Add Device Page - **Page Title**: Add New Device - **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device. - **Elements**:   - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.   - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.   - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).   - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).   - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 4. Device Control Page - **Page Title**: Device Control - **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings. - **Elements**:   - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.   - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.   - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).   - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.   - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.   - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.  ### 5. Automation Rules Page - **Page Title**: Automation Rules - **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.   - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.   - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.   - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).   - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).   - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.   - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).   - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. Energy Report Page - **Page Title**: Energy Report - **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.   - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.   - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.   - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.   - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Activity Logs Page - **Page Title**: Activity Logs - **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events. - **Elements**:   - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.   - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.   - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.   - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com   jane_smith|jane@example.com   ```  ### 2. Device Data - **File Name**: `devices.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|   john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00   jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|   ```  ### 3. Room Data - **File Name**: `rooms.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|room_id|room_name   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room   john_doe|2|Bedroom   john_doe|3|Kitchen   jane_smith|1|Living Room   ```  ### 4. Automation Rules Data - **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true   john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true   jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true   ```  ### 5. Energy Consumption Logs - **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5   john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3   john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6   jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2   ```  ### 6. Activity Logs - **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|timestamp|device_id|action|details   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights   john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72   jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# SmartHomeManager Flask Templates and Element IDs Specification

This document details all Flask HTML templates, their container IDs, element IDs, and related navigation for the SmartHomeManager application as per user task description.

---

## 1. Dashboard Page
- **Template file path:** templates/dashboard.html
- **Page Title (h1):** Overview
- **Main container ID:** dashboard-page
- **Elements:**
  - Div ID: device-summary (shows total devices, online devices, offline devices)
  - Button ID: devices-button (navigate to Device List page)
  - Button ID: automation-button (navigate to Automation Rules page)
  - Button ID: energy-button (navigate to Energy Report page)
  - Button ID: activity-button (navigate to Activity Logs page)

## 2. Device List Page
- **Template file path:** templates/devices/list.html
- **Page Title (h1):** My Devices
- **Main container ID:** device-list-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table ID: device-table (lists all devices)
  - Buttons:
    - add-device-button (navigate to Add Device page)
    - control-device-button-{device_id} (dynamic buttons on each device row to navigate to Device Control page; {device_id} replaced with actual device ID)

## 3. Add Device Page
- **Template file path:** templates/devices/add.html
- **Page Title (h1):** New Device
- **Main container ID:** add-device-page
- **Elements:**
  - Input ID: device-name (input field for device name)
  - Dropdown select ID: device-type (options: Light, Camera, Sensor, Thermostat)
  - Dropdown select ID: room-select (options: Living Room, Bedroom, Bathroom, etc.)
  - Button ID: submit-device-button (submit new device form)
  - Button ID: back-to-dashboard (navigate back to Dashboard page)

## 4. Device Control Page
- **Template file path:** templates/devices/control.html
- **Page Title (h1):** Device Control
- **Main container ID:** device-control-page
- **Elements:**
  - Text display ID: device-name-display (displays selected device name)
  - Text display ID: device-status-display (displays current device status: Online/Offline)
  - Button ID: power-toggle (toggle device power on/off)
  - Button ID: save-device-settings-button (save current settings)
  - Button ID: back-to-device-list (navigate back to Device List page)

## 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Template file path:** templates/automation.html
- **Page Title (h1):** Automation
- **Main container ID:** automation-page
- **Elements:**
  - Div ID: automation-container
  - Table ID: rules-table (lists all automation rules)
  - Input ID: rule-name-input (input for rule name)
  - Select ID: trigger-type-select (options: Time, Temperature, Motion, etc.)
  - Input ID: trigger-value (input for trigger value or threshold)
  - Select ID: action-device-select (to select target device)
  - Select ID: action-type-select (options: Turn On/Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature)
  - Button ID: add-rule-button (add new automation rule)
  - Button ID: back-to-dashboard-button (navigate back to Dashboard page)

## 6. Energy Report Page
- **Template file path:** templates/reports.html
- **Page Title (h1):** Energy Consumption Report
- **Main container ID:** energy-page
- **Elements:**
  - Div ID: energy-summary (summary of energy consumption)
  - Input ID: date-filter (filter energy data by date)
  - Button ID: apply-filter-button (apply energy date filter)
  - Button ID: back-to-dashboard-button (navigate back to Dashboard page)

## 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Template file path:** templates/activity.html
- **Page Title (h1):** Activity Logs
- **Main container ID:** activity-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table ID: activity-logs-table (logs showing timestamp, device, action, details)
  - Input ID: search-filter-input (filter activity logs)
  - Button ID: search-button (execute search filter)
  - Button ID: clear-filter-button (clear search filter)
  - Button ID: back-to-dashboard-button (navigate back to Dashboard page)

---

## Navigation Mapping using `url_for()` (Flask)

| Button ID                   | Navigation Target            | url_for Function                  |
|-----------------------------|-----------------------------|----------------------------------|
| devices-button              | Device List Page             | `url_for('list_devices')`          |
| automation-button           | Automation Page             | `url_for('automation_page')`       |
| energy-button              | Energy Report Page          | `url_for('reports_page')`          |
| activity-button            | Activity Logs Page          | `url_for('activity_page')`         |
| add-device-button          | Add Device Page             | `url_for('add_device')`            |
| back-to-dashboard (multiple pages) | Dashboard Page       | `url_for('dashboard_page')`        |
| back-to-device-list         | Device List Page             | `url_for('list_devices')`          |
| control-device-button-{id}  | Device Control Page          | `url_for('control_device', device_id={id})` |

---

## Notes
- Dynamic element IDs such as `control-device-button-{device_id}` will have `{device_id}` replaced with the specific device id.
- All IDs use kebab-case consistent with user task description.
- Page titles match exactly the requested titles.

This specification should be the single source of truth for front-end implementation of Flask templates and their element IDs in 'SmartHomeManager'.

User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com   jane_smith|jane@example.com   ```  ### 2. Device Data - **File Name**: `devices.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|   john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00   jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|   ```  ### 3. Room Data - **File Name**: `rooms.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|room_id|room_name   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room   john_doe|2|Bedroom   john_doe|3|Kitchen   jane_smith|1|Living Room   ```  ### 4. Automation Rules Data - **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true   john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true   jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true   ```  ### 5. Energy Consumption Logs - **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5   john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3   john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6   jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2   ```  ### 6. Activity Logs - **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|timestamp|device_id|action|details   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights   john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72   jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

  - Div ID: energy-summary (summary of energy consumption)
  - Input ID: date-filter (filter energy data by date)
  - Button ID: apply-filter-button (apply energy date filter)
  - Button ID: back-to-dashboard-button (navigate back to Dashboard page)

## 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Template file path:** templates/activity.html
- **Page Title (h1):** Activity Logs
- **Main container ID:** activity-page
- **Elements:**
  - Table ID: activity-logs-table (logs showing timestamp, device, action, details)
  - Input ID: search-filter-input (filter activity logs)
  - Button ID: search-button (execute search filter)
  - Button ID: clear-filter-button (clear search filter)
  - Button ID: back-to-dashboard-button (navigate back to Dashboard page)

---

## Navigation Mapping using `url_for()` (Flask)

| Button ID                   | Navigation Target            | url_for Function                  |
|-----------------------------|-----------------------------|----------------------------------|
| devices-button              | Device List Page             | `url_for('list_devices')`          |
| automation-button           | Automation Page             | `url_for('automation_page')`       |
| energy-button              | Energy Report Page          | `url_for('reports_page')`          |
| activity-button            | Activity Logs Page          | `url_for('activity_page')`         |
| add-device-button          | Add Device Page             | `url_for('add_device')`            |
| back-to-dashboard (multiple pages) | Dashboard Page       | `url_for('dashboard_page')`        |
| back-to-device-list         | Device List Page             | `url_for('list_devices')`          |
| control-device-button-{id}  | Device Control Page          | `url_for('control_device', device_id={id})` |

---

- Dynamic element IDs such as `control-device-button-{device_id}` will have `{device_id}` replaced with the specific device id.
- All IDs use kebab-case consistent with user task description.
- Page titles match exactly the requested titles.

This specification should be the single source of truth for front-end implementation of Flask templates and their element IDs in 'SmartHomeManager'.
